	// Rewrite of Skeleton Wraith King Vampiric Aura
	  // Author: Noya
	  // Date: 12.1.2015.
	  // Notes: Using the datadriven Lifesteal Action (shows a +Healed green popup)
	"demonhunter_vampiric_aura"
	  {
		// General
